QuantAlgo.W4A8_MXFP4_INT8 == 'W4A8_MXFP4_INT8'\n\n    def test_quant_mode_has_w4a8_mxfp4_int8_flag(self):\n        \"\"\"Verify W4A8_MXFP4_INT8 flag exists in QuantMode.\"\"\"\n        assert hasattr(QuantMode, 'W4A8_MXFP4_INT8')\n        # Verify it's a unique flag with its own bit position\n        mode = QuantMode.W4A8_MXFP4_INT8\n        assert mode.value != 0\n        # Ensure it doesn't conflict with other MXFP4 modes\n        assert mode != QuantMode.W4A8_MXFP4_FP8\n        assert mode != QuantMode.W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8\n        assert mode != QuantMode.W4A16_MXFP4\n\n    def test_has_w4a8_mxfp4_int8_method(self):\n        \"\"\"Test has_w4a8_mxfp4_int8() method.\"\"\"\n        mode_with_int8 = QuantMode.from_description(use_w4a8_mxfp4_int8=True)\n        assert mode_with_int8.has_w4a8_mxfp4_int8()\n\n        mode_without_int8 = QuantMode.from_description()\n        assert not mode_without_int8.has_w4a8_mxfp4_int8()\n\n        # Verify it's orthogonal to other MXFP4 modes\n        fp8_mode = QuantMode.from_description(use_w4a8_mxfp4_fp8=True)\n        assert not fp8_mode.has_w4a8_mxfp4_int8()\n        assert fp8_mode.has_w4a8_mxfp4_fp8()\n\n    def
